---
title     : "Typed: Raw terms with types (broken)"
layout    : page
permalink : /Typed
---

This version uses raw terms. Substitution presumes that no
generation of fresh names is required.

The substitution algorithm is based on one by McBride.
It is given a map from names to terms. Say the mapping of a
name is trivial if it takes a name to a term consisting of
just the variable with that name. No fresh names are required
if the mapping on each variable is either trivial or to a
closed term. However, the proof of correctness currently
contains a hole, and may be difficult to repair.

## Values do not reduce

Values do not reduce.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Val-⟶"></a><a id="11763" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11763" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="11769" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11771" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="11773" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11774" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11774" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="11776" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11776" class="Bound">N</a><a id="11777" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11779" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11781" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#7930" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="11787" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11774" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="11789" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11791" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="11793" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11794" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11774" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="11796" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#8197" class="Datatype Operator">⟶</a> <a id="11798" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11776" class="Bound">N</a><a id="11799" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="11801" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11763" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="11807" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#8080" class="InductiveConstructor">Fun</a> <a id="11811" class="Symbol">()</a>
<a id="11814" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11763" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="11820" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#7958" class="InductiveConstructor">Zero</a> <a id="11825" class="Symbol">()</a>
<a id="11828" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11763" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="11834" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11835" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#8003" class="InductiveConstructor">Suc</a> <a id="11839" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11839" class="Bound">VM</a><a id="11841" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11843" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11844" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#8512" class="InductiveConstructor">ξ-suc</a> <a id="11850" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11850" class="Bound">M⟶N</a><a id="11853" class="Symbol">)</a>  <a id="11856" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="11859" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11763" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="11865" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11839" class="Bound">VM</a> <a id="11868" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11850" class="Bound">M⟶N</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

As a corollary, terms that reduce are not values.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="⟶-Val"></a><a id="11947" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11947" class="Function">⟶-Val</a> <a id="11953" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11955" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="11957" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11958" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11958" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="11960" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11960" class="Bound">N</a><a id="11961" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11963" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11965" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11966" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11958" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="11968" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#8197" class="Datatype Operator">⟶</a> <a id="11970" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11960" class="Bound">N</a><a id="11971" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11973" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11975" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="11977" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#7930" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="11983" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11958" class="Bound">M</a>
<a id="11985" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11947" class="Function">⟶-Val</a> <a id="11991" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11991" class="Bound">M⟶N</a> <a id="11995" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11995" class="Bound">VM</a>  <a id="11999" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="12002" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11763" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="12008" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11995" class="Bound">VM</a> <a id="12011" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11991" class="Bound">M⟶N</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Reduction is deterministic

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="det"></a><a id="12071" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#12071" class="Function">det</a> <a id="12075" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12077" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="12079" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12080" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#12080" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="12082" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#12082" class="Bound">M′</a> <a id="12085" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#12085" class="Bound">M″</a><a id="12087" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="12091" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12093" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12094" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#12080" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="12096" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#8197" class="Datatype Operator">⟶</a> <a id="12098" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#12082" class="Bound">M′</a><a id="12100" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="12104" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12106" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12107" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#12080" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="12109" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#8197" class="Datatype Operator">⟶</a> <a id="12111" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#12085" class="Bound">M″</a><a id="12113" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="12119" class="Comment">----------</a>

<a id="13541" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#12071" class="Function">det</a> <a id="13545" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13546" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#9273" class="InductiveConstructor">β-Y</a> <a id="13550" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a><a id="13554" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13556" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13557" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#9201" class="InductiveConstructor">ξ-Y</a> <a id="13561" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#13561" class="Bound">M⟶M″</a><a id="13565" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13567" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13569" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Empty.html#360" class="Function">⊥-elim</a> <a id="13576" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13577" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11763" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="13583" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#8080" class="InductiveConstructor">Fun</a> <a id="13587" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#13561" class="Bound">M⟶M″</a><a id="13591" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="13593" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#12071" class="Function">det</a> <a id="13597" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13598" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#9273" class="InductiveConstructor">β-Y</a> <a id="13602" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a><a id="13606" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13608" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13609" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#9273" class="InductiveConstructor">β-Y</a> <a id="13613" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a><a id="13617" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13619" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13621" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Almost half the lines in the above proof are redundant, for example

    det (ξ-·₁ L⟶L′) (ξ-·₂ VL _) = ⊥-elim (Val-⟶ VL L⟶L′)
    det (ξ-·₂ VL _) (ξ-·₁ L⟶L″) = ⊥-elim (Val-⟶ VL L⟶L″)
 
are essentially identical. What we might like to do is delete the
redundant lines and add

    det M⟶M′ M⟶M″ = sym (det M⟶M″ M⟶M′)

to the bottom of the proof. But this does not work. The termination
checker complains, because the arguments have merely switched order
and neither is smaller.

## Canonical forms

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14149" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Canonical"></a><a id="14154" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#14154" class="Datatype">Canonical</a> <a id="14164" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14166" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#1725" class="Datatype">Term</a> <a id="14171" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14173" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#1590" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="14178" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14180" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="14184" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="Canonical.Zero"></a><a id="14193" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#14193" class="InductiveConstructor">Zero</a> <a id="14198" class="Symbol">:</a> 
      <a id="14207" class="Comment">-------------------</a>
      <a id="14233" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#14154" class="Datatype">Canonical</a> <a id="14243" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#1850" class="InductiveConstructor">`zero</a> <a id="14249" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#1609" class="InductiveConstructor">`ℕ</a>

  <a id="Canonical.Suc"></a><a id="14255" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#14255" class="InductiveConstructor">Suc</a> <a id="14259" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14261" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="14263" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14264" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#14264" class="Bound">V</a><a id="14265" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="14271" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14273" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#14154" class="Datatype">Canonical</a> <a id="14283" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#14264" class="Bound">V</a> <a id="14285" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#1609" class="InductiveConstructor">`ℕ</a>
      <a id="14294" class="Comment">----------------------</a>

## Preservation

### Domain of an environment

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="16705" class="Comment">{-
dom : Env → List Id
dom ε            =  []
dom (Γ , x `: A)  =  x ∷ dom Γ

dom-lemma : ∀ {Γ y B} → Γ ∋ y `: B → y ∈ dom Γ
dom-lemma Z           =  here
dom-lemma (S x≢y ⊢y)  =  there (dom-lemma ⊢y)

free-lemma : ∀ {Γ M A} → Γ ⊢ M `: A → free M ⊆ dom Γ
free-lemma (Ax ⊢x) w∈ with w∈
...                      | here         =  dom-lemma ⊢x
...                      | there ()   
free-lemma {Γ} (⊢λ {N = N} ⊢N)          =  ∷-to-\\ (free-lemma ⊢N)
free-lemma (⊢L · ⊢M) w∈ with ++-to-⊎ w∈
...                        | inj₁ ∈L    = free-lemma ⊢L ∈L
...                        | inj₂ ∈M    = free-lemma ⊢M ∈M
free-lemma ⊢zero ()
free-lemma (⊢suc ⊢M) w∈                 = free-lemma ⊢M w∈
free-lemma (⊢pred ⊢M) w∈                = free-lemma ⊢M w∈
free-lemma (⊢if0 ⊢L ⊢M ⊢N) w∈
        with ++-to-⊎ w∈
...         | inj₁ ∈L                   = free-lemma ⊢L ∈L
...         | inj₂ ∈MN with ++-to-⊎ ∈MN
...                       | inj₁ ∈M     = free-lemma ⊢M ∈M
...                       | inj₂ ∈N     = free-lemma ⊢N ∈N
free-lemma (⊢Y ⊢M) w∈                   = free-lemma ⊢M w∈       
-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

<a id="19759" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#18686" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="19766" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#19766" class="Bound">⊢ρ</a> <a id="19769" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19770" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#2957" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢Y</a> <a id="19773" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#19773" class="Bound">⊢M</a><a id="19775" class="Symbol">)</a>                <a id="19792" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="19795" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#2957" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢Y</a> <a id="19798" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19799" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#18686" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="19806" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#19766" class="Bound">⊢ρ</a> <a id="19809" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#19773" class="Bound">⊢M</a><a id="19811" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Let's look at examples.  Assume `M` is closed.  Example 1.

    subst (∅ , "x" ↦ M) (`λ "y" `→ ` "x")  ≡  `λ "y" `→ M

Example 2.

      subst (∅ , "y" ↦ ` "y" , "x" ↦ M) (`λ "y" `→ ` "x" · ` "y")
    ≡
      `λ "y" `→ subst (∅ , "y" ↦ ` "y" , "x" ↦ M , "y" ↦ ` "y") (` "x" · ` "y")
    ≡
      `λ "y" `→ (M · ` "y")

The hypotheses of the theorem appear to be violated. Drat!
